invade_teschin = {
	allowed = {
		is_tatry_region = yes
	}
	available = {
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 8
			LEM = { exists = no }
			SCZ = { exists = no }
			TYM = { exists = no }
			ZGR = { exists = no }
			AND = {
				GUR = { exists = no }
				ZKP = { exists = no }
			}
			CIE = { exists = no }
			BSK = { exists = no }
			BBA = { exists = no }
			WYM = { exists = no }
		}
		country_exists = TSZ
		OR = {
			TSZ = { controls_state = 522 }
			TSZ = { controls_state = 925 }
			TSZ = { controls_state = 749 }
			TSZ = { controls_state = 784 }
			TSZ = { controls_state = 785 }
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1000
	}
	remove_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = TSZ
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		TSZ = {
			delete_unit = {}
		}			
	}
}

annex_podbeskidzie = {
	allowed = {
		is_tatry_region = yes
		NOT = {
			original_tag = BBA
			original_tag = WYM
		}
	}
	available = {
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 7
			LEM = { exists = no }
			SCZ = { exists = no }
			TYM = { exists = no }
			ZGR = { exists = no }
			GUR = { exists = no }
			ZKP = { exists = no }
			CIE = { exists = no }
			BSK = { exists = no }
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1000
	}
	remove_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BBA
				BBA = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
			}
		annex_country = {
			target = BBA
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BBA
				BBA = { NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT } }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BBA
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = WYM
				WYM = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
			}
		annex_country = {
			target = WYM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = WYM
				WYM = { NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT } }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WYM
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}				
	}
}


#BESKIDZKIE - FAZA DRUGA
carpathian_wars = { #
 icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
 allowed = {
 	is_tatry_region = yes
 	NOT = {
 		original_tag = TSZ
 	}
 }
 
 ai_will_do = {
 	factor = 100
 	modifier = {
 		factor = -110
 		FROM = {
 			original_tag = LEM
 		}
 		ROOT = { original_tag = GUR }
 		SCZ = { exists = yes }
 	}
 }
 
 available = {
 	date > 2028.02.01
 	has_war = no
 	FROM = {
 		is_neighbor_of = ROOT
 	}
 	ROOT = { NOT = { has_idea = cooldown } }
 }
 
 targets = {
 	BBA WYM CIE BSK GUR ZKP ZGR LEM SCZ TYM
 }
 
 target_trigger = {
 	FROM = {
 		is_neighbor_of = ROOT
		 NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
		 NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
 	}
 }
 war_with_target_on_complete = yes
 days_remove = 7
 
 complete_effect = {
 	ROOT = { add_timed_idea = {
 		idea = cooldown
 		days = 9
 	}
  }
 }
 remove_effect = {
 	declare_war_on = {
 		target = FROM
 		type = voivodeship_war
 	}
 }

}

#╚══════╝╚═╝░░╚═╝░╚═════╝░╚══════╝╚══════╝╚═════╝░╚═╝╚══════╝  ╚═╝ ░╚════╝░░╚═════╝░╚═╝░░╚═╝╚═╝░░╚═╝
#ZAGŁĘBIE I JURA - FAZA PIERWSZA


 jura_JWK = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JUR
			original_tag = CCH
			original_tag = JWK
		}		
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JUR
			original_tag = CCH
		}
		OR = {
			JUR = { exists = no }
			CCH = { exists = no }
		}			
		NOT = { 
			has_idea = cooldown
		}
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = JWK } }
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.02.14
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = JWK
	complete_effect = {
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 15
		}
	}
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision jura_JWK"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = JWK }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = JWK
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

#ZAGŁĘBIE I JURA - FAZA DRUGA


 zaglebie_war_1 = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JWK
			original_tag = JUR
			original_tag = CCH
		}
	}

	available = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = JWK
				original_tag = JUR
				original_tag = CCH
			}

			count_triggers = {
			amount = 3
				BRZ = { exists = no }
				JWK = { exists = no }
				JUR = { exists = no }
				CCH = { exists = no }
			}
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100

	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 21
	remove_effect  = {	
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision zaglebie_war_1"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = DGR
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = DGR }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = DGR }}
			 } 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = DGR
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = DGA
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = DGA }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = DGA }}
			 } 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = DGA
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = BED
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = BED }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = BED }}
			 } 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BED
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = SIE
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SIE }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = SIE }}
			 } 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SIE
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}									
			if = { limit = { country_exists = SOS 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SOS }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = SOS }}			
			} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SOS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = JAW
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = JAW }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAW }}			
			 } 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = JAW
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = ZAW
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZAW }}
			ROOT = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ZAW }}			
			 } 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ZAW
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

 invade_zaglebie_puppets = {
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = SOS
			original_tag = JAW
			original_tag = ZAW
			original_tag = JUR
			original_tag = JWK
			original_tag = CCH
		}
	}
	available = {
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 7
			DGR = { exists = no }
			SOS = { exists = no }
			JAW = { exists = no }
			ZAW = { exists = no }
			JUR = { exists = no }
			JWK = { exists = no }	
			CCH = { exists = no }
			BRZ = { exists = no }
		}
		SIE = { exists = yes }
		BED = { exists = yes }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1000
	}
	remove_effect = {
		if = {

		}
		}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {

		}
 	}
 }

silesian_war = { 
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war

	allowed = {
		is_upper_silesia = yes
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	visible = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = unified_voivodeship }
	}
	available = {
		date > 2028.04.01
		has_war = no
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
		}
		has_global_flag = chosen_silesian_behemoth
		ROOT = { NOT = { has_idea = cooldown }}
	}

	targets = {
		ASG RAS CHO RUD FER GLI TRC KAT SBW SOL DUR TYS JSW WOD
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
			NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		}
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	days_remove = 7
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 9
		}
	 }
	}
	remove_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}

}

			original_tag = BOH

		}
	}

		has_war = no

	}

		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14

		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision GAL_01_SALT_HYPERWAR"

				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = UMN }
					country_exists = BOH 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BOH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = BOH }
					country_exists = UMN 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = UMN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

				}

					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = WND 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = WND } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = WND
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = UJG

					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}

						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = HAB } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = HAB
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}				
		}

		}

						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = TRW

			target = TRW
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}

						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = BRS 
						 is_in_faction_with = BRS } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = BRS

		}

#PODKARPACKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA

 CHR_LEZ_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = CHR
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		country_exists = LEZ
		date > 2027.09.01
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision lezajsk_wypij_do_dna"
		if = { limit = { country_exists = LEZ }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = LEZ
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

 podkarpacie_TAR = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = LGP
			original_tag = UHR
			original_tag = UPA
			original_tag = CHR
			original_tag = RZE
			original_tag = KOZ
			original_tag = BSC
			original_tag = KRO
		}
	}

	available = {
		NOT = { 
			has_idea = cooldown
		}
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = TAR } }
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.04.20
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100

	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 10
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 11
		}
	 }
	}
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision podkarpacie_TAR"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = TAR }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TAR
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = KOL }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KOL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}				
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

#PODKARPACKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA

 heart_of_darkness = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	allowed = {
		is_subcarpathia = yes		
	}	
	available = {
		has_war = no
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 14
			KOL = { exists = no }
			LEZ = { exists = no }
			ANC = { exists = no }
			JSO = { exists = no }
			KRO = { exists = no }
			TAR = { exists = no }	
			UPA = { exists = no }
			KOZ = { exists = no }
			BSC = { exists = no }
			UHR = { exists = no }
			LGP = { exists = no }
			CHR = { exists = no }	
			RZE = { exists = no }	
			DBI = { exists = no }	
			MIE = { exists = no }	
			LCZ = { exists = no }
		}
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = BEX } }
	}


	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 10
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision heart_of_darkness"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = BEX }
			annex_country = {
				target = BEX
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_ai = yes } }
				news_event = {
					id = sanok.1
				}
			}
			}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

				amount = 12

#██║░░██║╚█████╔╝███████╗░░░██║░░░  ╚█████╔╝██║░░██║╚█████╔╝██████╔╝██████╔╝
#╚═╝░░╚═╝░╚════╝░╚══════╝░░░╚═╝░░░  ░╚════╝░╚═╝░░╚═╝░╚════╝░╚═════╝░╚═════╝░
#ŚWIĘTOKRZYSKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 holy_cross_KEL = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = KIE
			original_tag = NSZ
			original_tag = STO
			original_tag = NRA
			original_tag = STA
			original_tag = SND					
		}
	}

	available = {
		NOT = { 
			has_idea = cooldown
		}
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = KEL } }
		has_war = no
		NOT = { has_war_with = KEL}
		date > 2028.02.18
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = -1
			surrender_progress > 0.25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = -1
			original_tag = KIE
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 2
				NSZ = { exists = yes }
				STO = { exists = yes }
				NRA = { exists = yes }
			}
		}		
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = KEL
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 15
		}
	}
	}
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision holy_cross_KEL"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = KEL }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KEL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			}
	}

	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

 CRN_west_lublin_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_lubelskie = yes
			}

	visible = { original_tag = CRN }

	available = {				#wiem że przez to jest burdel w decyzjach ale wolę żeby było widoczne, przynajmniej na razie
		original_tag = CRN
		date > 2028.03.01
		#lubelskie data startu (to po to żebym mógł łatwiej wyszukać i zmieniać do balansowania)
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100

	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 15
	war_with_on_remove = PUL
	war_with_on_remove = KSN
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision CRN_west_lublin_war"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PUL
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = PUL
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PUL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = KSN
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = KSN
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KSN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

 CRN_east_lublin_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_lubelskie = yes
			}

	visible = { original_tag = CRN }

	available = {
		original_tag = CRN
		NOT = { country_exists = PUL }
		NOT = { country_exists = KSN }
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100

	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = SWD
	war_with_on_remove = ZUK
	war_with_on_remove = BIL
	war_with_on_remove = LEN
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision CRN_east_lublin_war"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SWD
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ZUK
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = BIL
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		declare_war_on = {

 RADOM_02_EAST_RADOM_WAR = {
	
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = AIR
			original_tag = PAB
			original_tag = SKA
			original_tag = CZA
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.11.01
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision wojna na wschodniej radomszczyznie"
		if = { limit = { country_exists = AIR
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = AIR 
						 is_in_faction_with = AIR } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = AIR
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = PAB
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = PAB 
						 is_in_faction_with = PAB } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = PAB
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SKA
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SKA
						 is_in_faction_with = SKA } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SKA
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = CZA
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CZA 
						 is_in_faction_with = CZA } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CZA
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}						
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

#RADOMSKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA
 RADOM_03_RADOM_WAR = {
	
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_radom_province = yes
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2029.05.01
		RAD = { has_country_flag = radom_committed }
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision wojna na radomszczyznie"
		if = { limit = { country_exists = AIR
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = AIR 
						 is_in_faction_with = AIR } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = AIR
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = PAB
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = PAB 
						 is_in_faction_with = PAB } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = PAB
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SKA
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SKA
						 is_in_faction_with = SKA } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SKA
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = CZA
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CZA 
						 is_in_faction_with = CZA } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CZA
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SAT
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SAT 
						 is_in_faction_with = SAT } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SAT
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SZY
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SZY 
						 is_in_faction_with = SZY } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SZY
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = APC
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = APC
						 is_in_faction_with = APC } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = APC
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}	
		if = { limit = { country_exists = GRJ
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = GRJ
						 is_in_faction_with = GRJ
						GRJ = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GRJ
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}	
		if = { limit = { country_exists = VRC
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = VRC
						 is_in_faction_with = VRC
						VRC = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = VRC
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }


 annex_radom = {
	allowed = {
		is_radom_province = yes
	}
	available = {
		has_country_flag = unified_voivodeship
		has_subject = RAD
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 30
	cost = 50
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1000
	}
	remove_effect = {
		annex_country = {
			target = RAD
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
 }

			original_tag = ZHP
			original_tag = ZYD
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.03.01
		OR = {
			original_tag = BBW
			original_tag = KRS
			original_tag = SAP
			AND = {
				original_tag = WML
				NOT = {
				country_exists = BBW
				country_exists = KRS
				country_exists = SAP
				country_exists = ZHP
				country_exists = ZYD
				}
			}
			original_tag = ZHP
			original_tag = ZYD
		}
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
		}
		ROOT = { NOT = { has_idea = cooldown } }
	}

	targets = {
		KAR TIG AMW RDM LKS RUT POG
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
			NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		}
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 9
		}
	 }
	}
	days_remove = 7
	remove_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}

	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}

 }

			}
		}

	available = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TVP
				original_tag = TVN
			}
			has_war = no
			date > 2028.04.11 #Nie wiem kiedy dobrze by było zacząć, więc roboczo jest tutaj
			is_in_faction = no
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {

					country_exists = TVN 
					}

				target = TVN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}

					country_exists = TVP 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TVP
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {

			has_war = yes
		}
	}

WARSZAWA_total_war= { # lewo/prawo

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_capital_district = yes
	}

	available = {
		is_capital_district = yes
		has_war = no
		date > 2033.03.01 #placeholder
	}
	cost = 1

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision WARSZAWA_centrum_battle_royale"
		if = { limit = { country_exists = ZYR
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZYR
					 is_in_faction_with = ZYR
					ZYR = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ZYR
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = GRD
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = GRD
					 is_in_faction_with = GRD
					GRD = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GRD
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = JEH
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = JEH
					 is_in_faction_with = JEH
					JEH = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JEH
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = CPK
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CPK
					 is_in_faction_with = CPK
					CPK = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CPK
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = WBG

					WBG = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = WBG
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = LAS

					LAS = { is_puppet = yes } } } }

		if = { limit = { country_exists = ZNP

					ZNP = { is_puppet = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {

WARSZAWA_jaki_vs_mafia = { #wrc vs wol

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = WRC
			original_tag = WOL
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2031.07.15 #placeholder
		has_global_flag = warszawa_prawica_win
	}


	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision WARSZAWA_jaki_vs_mafia"
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = WRC }
					country_exists = WOL 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WOL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}

 end_of_popular_front = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = AGR
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.05.16
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision end_of_popular_front"
		AGR = {
		leave_faction = yes
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SDL
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }
	

	podlasie_plemiona = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		
		allowed = {
			is_podlasie = yes
			NOT = {
				is_podlasie_tribe = yes
				original_tag = AGR
				original_tag = SDL
			}
		}
		
		target_array = global.podlasie_tribes
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_podlasie_tribe = yes
			}
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = BOM
						original_tag = KON
						original_tag = TAT
						original_tag = BEL
						original_tag = SAN
						original_tag = LMZ
					}
					ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { is_podlasie_tribe = yes } }
					FROM = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }
					FROM = { exists = yes }
					date > 2027.10.01
					has_war = no
					NOT = { has_idea = cooldown }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = SDL
						original_tag = AGR
						}
					ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { is_podlasie_tribe = yes } }
					FROM = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }
					FROM = { exists = yes }	
					count_triggers = {
							amount = 7
							TAT = {exists = no}
							SAN = {exists = no}
							LMZ = {exists = no}
							BEL = {exists = no}
							BOM = {exists = no}
							KON = {exists = no}
							SDL = {exists = no}
							AGR = {exists = no}
					}
					has_war = no
					NOT = { has_idea = cooldown }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = cooldown
				days = 11
			}
		}
		remove_effect  = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [ROOT.GetName] fires decision podlasie_plemiona"
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = FROM
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}

 north_mazovia_war = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = POL
				original_tag = ORL
				original_tag = SAS
				original_tag = MAR
			}
		}

		available = {
			date > 2029.04.01
			has_war = no
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 4
		remove_effect  = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: Decision north_mazovia_war"
				if = { limit = { country_exists = ORL
								NOT = { has_war_with = ORL }
								 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ORL } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ORL
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = POL
							NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = POL } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = POL
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = SAS
							NOT = { has_war_with = SAS }
								 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SAS } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SAS
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = KUR 
						NOT = { has_war_with = KUR }
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = KUR } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KUR
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = ZWK
							NOT = { has_war_with = ZWK } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZWK } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ZWK
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = MAR
							NOT = { has_war_with = MAR } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MAR } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = MAR
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = PLO
							NOT = { has_war_with = PLO } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = PLO } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PLO
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = GOS
							NOT = { has_war_with = GOS } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = GOS } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GOS
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = SRP
							NOT = { has_war_with = SRP } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SRP } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SRP
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = SCH
							NOT = { has_war_with = SCH } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SCH } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SCH
					type = annex_everything
				}
				}				
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}

 russian_invasion = {
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	allowed = {

 anti_russian_front = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = WRM 
	}

	available = {
		OR = {				
			date > 2028.04.01
			has_war_with = ROS
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 5
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision anti_russian_front"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ROS
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { original_tag = ROS }
				}
				ROOT = { 
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROS }
				}
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: Deccing on [ROS.GetName]"
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}

#POMORSKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 POMGDA_gdansk_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = GDA
			original_tag = MPR
			original_tag = BOL
		}
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.03.05
		country_exists = GDA
		country_exists = MPR
		country_exists = BOL
		has_war = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	days_remove = 14

	war_with_on_remove = GDA
	war_with_on_remove = MPR
	war_with_on_remove = BOL

	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision POMGDA_gdansk_war"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = GDA
					has_war_with = GDA
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GDA
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = BOL
					has_war_with = BOL
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BOL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = MPR
					has_war_with = MPR
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MPR
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_war_with = GDA
					has_war_with = BOL
				}
				AND = {
					has_war_with = GDA
					has_war_with = MPR
				}
				AND = {
					has_war_with = MPR
					has_war_with = BOL
				}
			}
		}
	}
 }

#POMORSKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA
 POMGDA_pomorze_jednoczenie_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_pomerelia = yes
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 8
				HEL = { exists = no }
				OWS = { exists = no }
				GAY = { exists = no }
				RLE = { exists = no }
				KSZ = { exists = no }
				KSC = { exists = no }	
				GDA = { exists = no }
				BOL = { exists = no }
				MPR = { exists = no }
				KOR = { exists = no }
				CZL = { exists = no }
				LOT = { exists = no }	
			}
			date > 2029.06.01
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = unified_voivodeship }
		#has_war = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	days_remove = 14

	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision POMGDA_pomorze_jednoczenie_war"

			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = GDY

				}
				country_exists = GDY

				target = GDY
				type = voivodeship_war
			}

			}			
		}

		available = {
			#ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = EKW } }
			has_war = no

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 14
		war_with_on_remove = FRE

			log = "[GetDateText]: Decision zachpom_EKW_vs_FRE"

					target = FRE

				}
				}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {

					}

							ROOT = { original_tag = JAS }

					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
							country_exists = USP
							NOT = { country_exists = JAS }
							ROOT = { original_tag = NOR }
					}
					declare_war_on = {

				}
				else_if = {

					}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = CAL
		}

		available = {
			date > 2028.09.01
			NOT = {
				country_exists = GNI
			}
			OR = {
				country_exists = KNN
				AND = {
					country_exists = KLO
					KLO = {
						is_subject = no
					}
				}
			}
			has_war = no
		}

		

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes

		war_with_on_remove = KLO
		war_with_on_remove = KNN

			log = "[GetDateText]: Decision CAL_gniezno_cleanup"

				limit = {
					country_exists = KNN
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KNN
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = KLO
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KLO
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}

 		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
 		}
	}

#KALISKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA
 barbarian_raid = {
	allowed = {
		always = yes
	}
	visible = {
		has_idea = barbarians_idea
		CAL = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = CAL_empire_or_death
				has_completed_focus = CAL_adapt_or_perish
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = CAL_barbarians_win_flag
		}
	}
	target_array = root.neighbors
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			# NOT = {
			# 	has_war = yes
			# }
			is_somsiad = no
			NOT = {
				original_tag = ZON
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				original_tag = WIZ
				original_tag = SAX
				original_tag = OST
				original_tag = JUT
				original_tag = FRK
				original_tag = HNN
				original_tag = SCY
				original_tag = AES
				original_tag = VAN
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = CAL
					original_tag = PRT
				}
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = CAL_empire_or_death
					OR = {
						ROOT = {
							tag = JUT
						}
						ROOT = {
							tag = HNN
						}
						ROOT = {
							tag = VAN
						}
						
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
	}

	remove_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
 }

	allowed = {

		country_exists = LIS

	available = {

			is_subject = no
		}
	}

		factor = 1000
	}
	complete_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = LIS
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
 }

#██║░░░░░██╔══╝░░██║░░╚██╗██║╚████║██║██║░░██╗██╔═██╗░██║██╔══╝░░
#███████╗███████╗╚██████╔╝██║░╚███║██║╚█████╔╝██║░╚██╗██║███████╗
#╚══════╝╚══════╝░╚═════╝░╚═╝░░╚══╝╚═╝░╚════╝░╚═╝░░╚═╝╚═╝╚══════╝
#LEGNICKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 EKS_annex_ECO_BOG = { #a wiecie co kurwa, polosujmy

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = EKS
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.04.01
		country_exists = ECO
		country_exists = BOG
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision EKS_annex_EKS_BOG"
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ECO
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = BOG
					transfer_troops = yes
				}				
			}
			20 = {
				ECO = {
					annex_country = {
						target = EKS
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = BOG
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			10 = {
				BOG = {
					annex_country = {
						target = EKS
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = ECO
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = BOG_eurokom
				}
			}
		}

	}
	
 }
#LEGNICKIE - FAZA DRUGA
 EKS_KGH_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = EKS
			original_tag = BOG
			original_tag = ECO
		}
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.10.15
		country_exists = KGH
		has_war = no
	}


	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = KGH
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision EKS_KGH_war"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = KGH
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

 KGH_EKS_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = KGH
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.10.15
		OR = {
		country_exists = EKS
		country_exists = ECO
		country_exists = BOG
		}
		has_war = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = EKS
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision KGH_EKS_war"
		if = {
			limit = { EKS = { exists = yes }}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = EKS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ECO = { exists = yes }}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ECO
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BOG = { exists = yes }}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BOG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}				
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

 ZUL_ANA_MNL_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = ZUL
			original_tag = ANA
			original_tag = MNL
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.01.01
		NOT = { has_country_flag = unified_voivodeship }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 7
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: ZUL_ANA_MNL_war"
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ZUL
					ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZUL } }
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ZUL
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ZUL
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					country_exists = ANA 
					ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ANA } } 
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ANA
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ANA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					country_exists = MNL 
					ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MNL } } 
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = MNL
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = MNL
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }	
#WROCŁAWSKIE - FAZA DRUGA
 okamura_ZUL_conquest_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = CZE
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.02.16		
	}

			}
		}

	}

 wroclaw_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war

		original_tag = ANA
		}		
	}

	available = {
		date > 2029.01.01
		count_triggers = {
				amount = 4
					WRO = { exists = no }
					RYB = { exists = no }
					CZE = { exists = no }
					ZUL = { exists = no }
					MNL = { exists = no }
					ANA = { exists = no }
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision wroclaw_war"

			} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MNL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = WRO 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = WRO }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WRO
				type = annex_everything

			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = CZE 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CZE }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CZE
				type = annex_everything
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = RYB 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = RYB }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RYB
				type = annex_everything
			}
			}

				target = ANA
				type = annex_everything
			}
			}
							
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

#NYSKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 battle_of_nysa = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_opolskie = yes
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = NYS
			original_tag = LEH
			OR = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = LCH
					OPO = { exists = no }
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = OPO
					LCH = { exists = no }
				}				
			}
		}
		date > 2028.02.27
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100

	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_remove = 11
	remove_effect  = {	
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision opole_battle_of_nysa"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = NYS
							NOT = { has_war_with = NYS}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = NYS } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = NYS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = LEH 
			NOT = { has_war_with = LEH}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = LEH } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LEH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
 		}
 }

 opole_gotterdammerung = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_opolskie = yes
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 2029.06.01
				has_war = no
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					OPO = { exists = no }
					MNI = { exists = no }
					LCH = { exists = no }
					LEH = { exists = no }
					WND = { exists = no }
					NYS = { exists = no }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				date > 2028.08.01
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					OPO = { exists = no }
					MNI = { exists = no }
					LCH = { exists = no }
					LEH = { exists = no }
					WND = { exists = no }
					NYS = { exists = no }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	days_re_enable = 30
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision opole_gotterdammerung"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = NYS
							NOT = { has_war_with = NYS}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = NYS } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = NYS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = LEH 
			NOT = { has_war_with = LEH}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = LEH } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LEH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = LCH
							NOT = { has_war_with = LCH}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = LCH } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LCH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = OPO 
			NOT = { has_war_with = OPO}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = OPO } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = OPO
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = WAN
							NOT = { has_war_with = WAN}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = WAN } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WAN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = MNI 
			NOT = { has_war_with = MNI}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MNI } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MNI
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
 		}
